### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Can I buy gift cards with Bitcoin or crypto?

Yes, you can spend your crypto to purchase over 5,000+ gift cards from a variety of retailers, including Amazon, Apple, Walmart, Steam, Google Play etc.

### 

What gift card brands can I purchase with crypto?

You can shop gift cards for a variety of brands with cryptocurrency. Some of the most popular brands include Amazon, Starbucks, Walmart, Apple, Netflix, Airbnb, Uber, eBay, Roblox, Spotify, Free Fire etc.

### 

What cryptocurrencies can I use to shop gift cards?

At Bitrefill, you can purchase gift cards using a variety of cryptocurrencies including Bitcoin, Lightning, Ethereum, USDC, USDT, Binance Pay, Litecoin, Dogecoin, Solana or Dash.

### 

What crypto wallets/exchanges can I use to buy gift cards?

You can use several different wallets and exchanges to buy gift cards at Bitrefill. Some of the most popular options include Binance Pay, Coinbase, Kraken, Trust Wallet, Bitfinex, Blockchain, Edge, KuCoin, Ledger, Strike, Bitstamp etc.

### 

How does the crypto payment process work?

The process of paying with cryptocurrency is simple and straightforward.

1.  Select your gift card along with the desired value.
2.  Complete the required fields to proceed to the payment method.
3.  Choose your preferred cryptocurrency and send the corresponding amount to the provided cryptocurrency address or scan the QR code using your mobile wallet.
4.  Once the payment is made, the digital gift card code should arrive within a few moments and you will be emailed a copy too.

### 

How quickly will my gift card arrive after I order it?

If you order a gift card from our website, your digital gift card should arrive almost instantaneously after you order it. All gift cards are delivered via email too, so as soon as your order is processed, the gift card will be sent to the email address you provided.

### 

I paid for the gift card but didn’t receive it. What should I do?

We're sorry to hear that you didn't receive your gift card. Please reach out to our customer support team at [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and they will be more than happy to help you out.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

**One card. A world of possibilities!**

A Disney Gift Card eGift can be used for practically all things Disney! With just one card you can access the following products:

*   Disney+
*   Disney Bundle Subscription (incl. Disney+, Hulu, and ESPN+)
*   Disneystore.com
*   Physical Disney Stores in the US
*   Disney Parks and Resorts
*   Disney on Broadway (Lion king, Aladdin, Frozen, The Beauty and the Beast)
*   Disney Cruise Line

  
Buy Disney USD Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

How to Redeem your Disney Gift Card eGift:

**In-person**, present the barcode above to a Disney Cast Member at participating locations.

**Online**, enter the Disney Gift Card eGift number at checkout. The use of multiple cards per purchase may not be permitted for certain sites. Please contact the redemption location of your choice for more information. Please note: your Disney Gift Card EAN may be required for redemption. In-Store Mobile Redemption Instructions Recipient: To redeem your Disney Gift Card eGift from a mobile device, display the barcode, Gift Card Number, and associated EAN (if applicable) to the cashier at the time of purchase. Cashier: Scan the barcode off of the mobile device and/or hand key the Gift Card Number and associated EAN (if applicable) into the POS

### Terms and Conditions

[https://www.disneygiftcard.com/terms/us](https://www.disneygiftcard.com/terms/us)

**For users outside the US, this card cannot be used for Disney+ or Bundle Subscriptions.**

*   Redeemable for goods and services at participating Disney locations.
*   Not refundable or redeemable for cash unless required by law.
*   Not for resale.
*   Issued by, and represents a legal obligation solely of, Disney Gift Card Services, Inc.
*   Lost, damaged, or stolen cards may be replaced only if the original proof of purchase receipt and the complete card number is provided.
*   For card balance inquiries, call 1-877-650-4327 or visit disneygiftcard.com.
*   For complete terms and conditions (including arbitration agreement), visit [disneygiftcard.com](http://disneygiftcard.com/)
    .

userint95

Nov 05, 2025

If you call concierge you can use multiple gift cards to pay, we used 4 to pay for our entire trip. You cannot add them to be used with a magic band but you can scan the barcode in the park. These work awesome!! No issues at all. If you don’t want to call concierge than you can use the Disney gift cards website and merge the balances.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Disney USD accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Disney USD does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Disney USD gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Disney USD.

### 

How can I buy an Disney USD gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Disney USD gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Disney USD gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Disney USD gift card?

Once you have purchased an Disney USD gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Activitygift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/activitygift-us/)
, [Hello Yo](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/hello-yo-international/)
, [Likee](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/likee-international/)
, [LiveMe Coins](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/liveme-coins-international/)
 and [OSN+ 6 Months Subscription](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/osn_-6-months-subscription-algeria/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai.

### 

How can I buy an Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card?

Once you have purchased an Total War Shogun 2 Rise of the Samurai gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Diablo® IV Platinum can be exchanged to customize your in-game experience with purchasable cosmetic items from the Shop, used to unlock access to the premium Battle Pass, and Battle Pass Tier Skips.

Diablo® IV is the ultimate action RPG experience with endless evil to slaughter, countless abilities to master, nightmarish dungeons, and legendary loot. Embark on the campaign solo or with friends, meeting memorable characters through beautifully dark settings and a gripping story, or explore an expansive end game and shared world where players can meet in towns to trade, team up to battle world bosses, or descend into PVP zones to test their skills against other players – no lobbies necessary – with cross-play and cross-progression on all available platforms. For more information, visit www.diablo.com

  
Buy XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum accept Bitcoin or crypto?

XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum.

### 

How can I buy an XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card?

Once you have purchased an XBox: Diablo IV Global Platinum gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Monster Hunter: World accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Monster Hunter: World does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Monster Hunter: World gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Monster Hunter: World.

### 

How can I buy an Monster Hunter: World gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Monster Hunter: World gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Monster Hunter: World gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Monster Hunter: World gift card?

Once you have purchased an Monster Hunter: World gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Kinguin is the premier destination for all your digital gaming needs. Established in 2013, it offer a curated selection that caters to the diverse tastes of the gaming community.

**Discover a World of Games**

*   **95,000+ Titles**: From casual puzzles to hardcore adventures, our extensive library ensures that every gamer finds something to love.
*   **Top Brands & Games**: Explore popular titles from leading brands like **FIFA**, **Call of Duty**, **Minecraft**, and **Assassin's Creed**. Buy subscriptions such as **Discord Nitro**, **Spotify** and **NordVPN**.

**Why Shop on Kinguin**

*   **Extensive Game Library**:Discover over 95,000 games, ranging from popular titles to unique indie gems. Whether you're a casual gamer or a hardcore enthusiast, Kinguin has something for everyone.
*   **Competitive Pricing**: Enjoy great savings with competitive prices, exclusive deals, and frequent discounts, making it easier to expand your game collection without breaking the bank.
*   **Instant Access**: Receive your game keys immediately after purchase, so you can start playing without any waiting time
*   **Comprehensive Gaming Essentials**: Shop for more than just games—find DLCs, character skins, and essential software to enhance your gaming experience.

Choosing the Kinguin Games Store via Bitrefill adds an additional layer of convenience. Paying with crypto allows instant access to your code, facilitating immediate immersion into your digital experience.

  
Buy Kinguin Games Store EUR Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  To redeem your code, please visit this website: [http://www.kinguin.net/redeem](http://www.kinguin.net/redeem)
     (you need to be signed in to your account).
2.  Gift cards can be redeemed up to 100 days after the purchase.

### Terms and Conditions

Gift card can be redeemed up to 100 days after the purchase.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Kinguin Games Store EUR accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Kinguin Games Store EUR does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Kinguin Games Store EUR.

### 

How can I buy an Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card?

Once you have purchased an Kinguin Games Store EUR gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

 page for more FAQs

### 

Can I buy gift cards with Bitcoin or crypto?

Yes, you can spend your crypto to purchase over 5,000+ gift cards from a variety of retailers, including Amazon, Apple, Walmart, Steam, Google Play etc.

### 

What gift card brands can I purchase with crypto?

You can shop gift cards for a variety of brands with cryptocurrency. Some of the most popular brands include Amazon, Starbucks, Walmart, Apple, Netflix, Airbnb, Uber, eBay, Roblox, Spotify, Free Fire etc.

### 

What cryptocurrencies can I use to shop gift cards?

At Bitrefill, you can purchase gift cards using a variety of cryptocurrencies including Bitcoin, Lightning, Ethereum, USDC, USDT, Binance Pay, Litecoin, Dogecoin, Solana or Dash.

### 

What crypto wallets/exchanges can I use to buy gift cards?

You can use several different wallets and exchanges to buy gift cards at Bitrefill. Some of the most popular options include Binance Pay, Coinbase, Kraken, Trust Wallet, Bitfinex, Blockchain, Edge, KuCoin, Ledger, Strike, Bitstamp etc.

### 

How does the crypto payment process work?

The process of paying with cryptocurrency is simple and straightforward.

1.  Select your gift card along with the desired value.
2.  Complete the required fields to proceed to the payment method.
3.  Choose your preferred cryptocurrency and send the corresponding amount to the provided cryptocurrency address or scan the QR code using your mobile wallet.
4.  Once the payment is made, the digital gift card code should arrive within a few moments and you will be emailed a copy too.

### 

How quickly will my gift card arrive after I order it?

If you order a gift card from our website, your digital gift card should arrive almost instantaneously after you order it. All gift cards are delivered via email too, so as soon as your order is processed, the gift card will be sent to the email address you provided.

###

 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Save the bankers is a campaign to preserve the splendid way of life of the bankers of Wall Street. Rest assured Every satoshi that you use will go undiluted to the bankers!  

  
Buy Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### Terms and Conditions

By making a donation to “Save the Bankers”, you are contributing to the fundraising campaign better explained [here](https://www.savethebankers.com/)
. This campaign seeks to collect charitable contributions to help the Bankers of Wall Street survive their upcoming doom brought about by the rise of cryptocurrencies. By donating via this page you are sending your coins directly to Bitrefill. 100% of the coins collected in this context will be used (in their fiat equivalent at the time of conversion - they prefer cash) to fund the endangered lifestyle of bankers. Your donation will be anonymous unless you specifically ask to be named. Your donation is definitive, will not be refunded, and by donating you expressly represent that you are aware of the intended destination of such donations and you agree with the goals of the campaign. We want to stress that despite any humorous undertones you may detect, both the donation request and the intention to give it to bankers are actual features of this campaign. We thank you in advance for your kind contribution to this worthy cause. [General Terms and Conditions of Bitrefill](https://www.bitrefill.com/terms/)
 apply.

### 

Does Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers.

### 

How can I buy an Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card?

Once you have purchased an Save the bankers - For real friends of the bankers gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Can I buy gift cards with Bitcoin or crypto?

Yes, you can spend your crypto to purchase over 5,000+ gift cards from a variety of retailers, including Amazon, Apple, Walmart, Steam, Google Play etc.

### 

What gift card brands can I purchase with crypto?

You can shop gift cards for a variety of brands with cryptocurrency. Some of the most popular brands include Amazon, Starbucks, Walmart, Apple, Netflix, Airbnb, Uber, eBay, Roblox, Spotify, Free Fire etc.

### 

What cryptocurrencies can I use to shop gift cards?

At Bitrefill, you can purchase gift cards using a variety of cryptocurrencies including Bitcoin, Lightning, Ethereum, USDC, USDT, Binance Pay, Litecoin, Dogecoin, Solana or Dash.

### 

What crypto wallets/exchanges can I use to buy gift cards?

You can use several different wallets and exchanges to buy gift cards at Bitrefill. Some of the most popular options include Binance Pay, Coinbase, Kraken, Trust Wallet, Bitfinex, Blockchain, Edge, KuCoin, Ledger, Strike, Bitstamp etc.

### 

How does the crypto payment process work?

The process of paying with cryptocurrency is simple and straightforward.

1.  Select your gift card along with the desired value.
2.  Complete the required fields to proceed to the payment method.
3.  Choose your preferred cryptocurrency and send the corresponding amount to the provided cryptocurrency address or scan the QR code using your mobile wallet.
4.  Once the payment is made, the digital gift card code should arrive within a few moments and you will be emailed a copy too.

### 

How quickly will my gift card arrive after I order it?

If you order a gift card from our website, your digital gift card should arrive almost instantaneously after you order it. All gift cards are delivered via email too, so as soon as your order is processed, the gift card will be sent to the email address you provided.

### 

I paid for the gift card but didn’t receive it. What should I do?

We're sorry to hear that you didn't receive your gift card. Please reach out to our customer support team at [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and they will be more than happy to help you out.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### 

Does EA Access 1 Month accept Bitcoin or crypto?

EA Access 1 Month does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an EA Access 1 Month gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at EA Access 1 Month.

### 

How can I buy an EA Access 1 Month gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the EA Access 1 Month gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your EA Access 1 Month gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my EA Access 1 Month gift card?

Once you have purchased an EA Access 1 Month gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### Description

Apex Legends Coins prepaid card is the in-game currency can be used to purchase new skins for characters and weapons in the direct purchase shop. Apex Coins can also be used to purchase cosmetic Apex Packs and to unlock new characters through the in-game store.  

  
Buy Apex Legends Coins Origin Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

To redeem Apex Legends codes and get rewards, launch the game on your platform and navigate to the main menu.  
From there, find the \`Store\` or \`Shop\` option,  
Then select \`Redeem Code\`.  
Enter your code accurately, including any special characters, and confirm the redemption.  
Once the code is processed, your rewards will be added to your account, which you can check in your inventory or the relevant section of the game

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Apex Legends Coins Origin accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Apex Legends Coins Origin does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Apex Legends Coins Origin.

### 

How can I buy an Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card?

Once you have purchased an Apex Legends Coins Origin gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

 page for more FAQs

### 

Can I buy gift cards with Bitcoin or crypto?

Yes, you can spend your crypto to purchase over 5,000+ gift cards from a variety of retailers, including Amazon, Apple, Walmart, Steam, Google Play etc.

### 

What gift card brands can I purchase with crypto?

You can shop gift cards for a variety of brands with cryptocurrency. Some of the most popular brands include Amazon, Starbucks, Walmart, Apple, Netflix, Airbnb, Uber, eBay, Roblox, Spotify, Free Fire etc.

### 

What cryptocurrencies can I use to shop gift cards?

At Bitrefill, you can purchase gift cards using a variety of cryptocurrencies including Bitcoin, Lightning, Ethereum, USDC, USDT, Binance Pay, Litecoin, Dogecoin, Solana or Dash.

### 

What crypto wallets/exchanges can I use to buy gift cards?

You can use several different wallets and exchanges to buy gift cards at Bitrefill. Some of the most popular options include Binance Pay, Coinbase, Kraken, Trust Wallet, Bitfinex, Blockchain, Edge, KuCoin, Ledger, Strike, Bitstamp etc.

### 

How does the crypto payment process work?

The process of paying with cryptocurrency is simple and straightforward.

1.  Select your gift card along with the desired value.
2.  Complete the required fields to proceed to the payment method.
3.  Choose your preferred cryptocurrency and send the corresponding amount to the provided cryptocurrency address or scan the QR code using your mobile wallet.
4.  Once the payment is made, the digital gift card code should arrive within a few moments and you will be emailed a copy too.

### 

How quickly will my gift card arrive after I order it?

If you order a gift card from our website, your digital gift card should arrive almost instantaneously after you order it. All gift cards are delivered via email too, so as soon as your order is processed, the gift card will be sent to the email address you provided.

### 

I paid for the gift card but didn’t receive it. What should I do?

 and they will be more than happy to help you out.

 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Experience the magic of RuneScape, the world's most popular free-to-play game with the Jagex RuneScape International card. Revel in the vast, immersive world of Gielinor packed with numerous quests, diverse races, and thrilling adventures that promises a unique gaming experience.

*   **Membership:** Unlock hundreds of additional quests and an expanded game world.
*   **RuneCoins:** Used for in-game transactions, augment your gaming experience.
*   **Keys packages:** Gain access to all-new virtual features in RuneScape.
*   **Loyalty rewards:** Earn rewards that enhance your gameplay and comradeship within the RuneScape community.

  
Buy Jagex RuneScape Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

To purchase subscriptions and/or in-game items using the RuneScape Card:

1.  Go to [http://www.runescape.com/store\_locator.ws](http://www.runescape.com/store_locator.ws)
    
2.  Click "Activate Card"
3.  Log in when prompted
4.  Enter in your Digital PIN code
5.  Select which RuneScape package you want

Start Playing!

[https://www.jagex.com/en-GB/terms](https://www.jagex.com/en-GB/terms)

IMPORTANT - PLEASE READ THESE TERMS AND CONDITIONS This prepaid RuneScape PIN may be redeemed only through the website and only by US residents. The PIN allows you to purchase subscription and/or in-game items for RuneScape to the value of the PIN purchased on the date the PIN code is redeemed (subject to network and server availability) and is valid as long as Jagex continues to offer RuneScape. The value of subscriptions and in-game items for RuneScape may change over time. Certain RuneScape features are available only if you are over a certain age. Internet access is required to play RuneScape and you are responsible for your own telecommunications charges. Your computer must meet certain minimum system requirements to play RuneScape and these requirements may change. ### How gift cards work

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Jagex RuneScape accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Jagex RuneScape does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Jagex RuneScape gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Jagex RuneScape.

### 

How can I buy an Jagex RuneScape gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Jagex RuneScape gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Jagex RuneScape gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Jagex RuneScape gift card?

Once you have purchased an Jagex RuneScape gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Razer Gold is a unified virtual credit system embraced by gamers worldwide. By completing a simple recharge of your Razer Gold account you can enjoy in-game purchases across thousands of gaming and entertainment platforms. Buyers enjoy added value by earning Razer Silver, the exclusive rewards program for gamers.

*   **Steam:** Enhance your gaming experiences with in-game purchases on Steam.
*   **Nintendo:** Boost your Nintendo gaming with upgrades and more.
*   **Spotify:** Enrich your music moments with Spotify Premium subscriptions.
*   **Minecraft:** Unlock new experiences in the world of Minecraft.
*   **Fortnite:** Level up your Fortnite gameplay with upgrades and skins.

When you choose to purchase a Razer Gold gift card with Bitrefill, you're embracing the future of online shopping. Why? Because our service allows you to pay with cryptocurrency. This ensures the instant delivery of your digital code, with no need for registration.

Plus, it's a global service, allowing access from anywhere in the world. So why wait? Pay with crypto, get your code, and top up your card balance.

  
Buy Razer Gold USD Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

Recharge your **USD Razer Gold** account to purchase games, digital content, and services.

1.  Go to [gold.razer.com](https://gold.razer.com/)
     and log in to your Razer Gold account.
2.  Click on \[Reload Now\] and choose Razer Gold Gift Card as your payment method.
3.  Start using your Razer Gold to earn Razer Silver, or select \[Razer Gold\] with supported games, digital content, and services.

If you have trouble redeeming the Global PIN, contact

[Razer Gold customer service](https://gold.razer.com/ticket-inbox/submit)
 to change your account to Global.

### Terms and Conditions

**This card can only be used in USD accounts**. **The currency for a Razer Gold account is determined during account setup and cannot be changed afterward.**

By using this card, you agree to the Terms of Service and Privacy Policy of Razer Gold, available at gold.razer.com. Compatible software, hardware, and internet access are required. Ownership and risk transfer to the buyer upon purchase. Razer is not responsible for any loss or damage from lost or stolen cards, unauthorized use, or misuse.

This card is non-resalable, cannot be redeemed for cash, and is non-refundable and non-exchangeable, except as required by law. Razer and its affiliates, licensees, and licensors offer no express or implied warranties for this card, disclaiming any such warranties to the fullest extent permitted by law. Void where prohibited.

Content availability and pricing are subject to change. For customer support, visit [gold.razer.com](https://gold.razer.com/)
.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Razer Gold USD accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Razer Gold USD does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Razer Gold USD gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Razer Gold USD.

### 

How can I buy an Razer Gold USD gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Razer Gold USD gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Razer Gold USD gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Razer Gold USD gift card?

Once you have purchased an Razer Gold USD gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

[Nufferton](https://www.nufferton.com/)
 was founded in 2016 on one simple idea: to create a contemporary version of the nearly forgotten, but amazing pyjamas, made for the sheets... and the streets. The loungewear label was dreamed up in Stockholm, and perhaps it’s not a coincidence. Swedes spend more time at home than anyone in the world.

  
Buy Nufferton Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### Terms and Conditions

*   The voucher can be used from anywhere in the world, at [https://www.nufferton.com/](https://www.nufferton.com/)
    
*   Gift cards/Vouchers worth more than your purchase will retain any remaining value. The purchase value will be deducted with each use until the entire value has been redeemed.
*   As all orders are final sale, we are unable to retroactively apply a voucher code or gift card to your purchase if you have forgotten to apply it at checkout.

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Nufferton accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Nufferton does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Nufferton gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Nufferton.

### 

How can I buy an Nufferton gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Nufferton gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Nufferton gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Nufferton gift card?

Once you have purchased an Nufferton gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 accept Bitcoin or crypto?

RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013.

### 

How can I buy an RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card?

Once you have purchased an RaceRoom DTM Experience 2013 gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

EA Access brings you great EA games for a great price. Download and play an evolving collection of EA titles for Xbox One at any time in The Vault.  

  
Buy EA Access 12 Months Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

NO EXPIRATION DATE AND NO SERVICE FEE REDEEM CODE: 1. Go to microsoft.com/redeem  
2\. Enter your code  
3\. Start shopping To create a new Microsoft account or read the full conditions (which can change without prior notice), go to microsoft.com/cardterms. (Code cannot be replaced - please keep in a safe place)

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does EA Access 12 Months accept Bitcoin or crypto?

EA Access 12 Months does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an EA Access 12 Months gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at EA Access 12 Months.

### 

How can I buy an EA Access 12 Months gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the EA Access 12 Months gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your EA Access 12 Months gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my EA Access 12 Months gift card?

Once you have purchased an EA Access 12 Months gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

Yalla Ludo, an app with voice chat, allows you to play Ludo or Domino with your friends online.  
Real time voice chat  
Talk with players via voice chat at any time, meet new friends, and enjoy the game!  
Various game modes  
Ludo includes two modes: 2&4 Players mode, Team mode. Each mode has four gameplays: Classic, Master, Quick, and Magic.  
Domino: Draw Game and All Five  
Play with friends easily. Private rooms and local rooms enable you to play with buddies either online or offline. Come and have fun in games together!  
Group Voice Chat for Gamers  
The chat room allows you to meet more gamers from all over the world and exchange ideas about games. You can also invite friends or others to play Ludo & Domino via this group chat.

  
Buy Yalla Ludo Diamond Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Locate the 12-digit PIN code.
2.  Go to the Yalla website through any internet browser on your PC or Smartphone.
3.  Enter the Yalla Ludo ID of the account you want to recharge.
4.  Choose the Recharge Amount that matches your Gift Card’s value.
5.  Enter your Gift Card’s 12-digit PIN code in the box shown.
6.  Click Redeem.
7.  And Enjoy!

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Yalla Ludo Diamond accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Yalla Ludo Diamond does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Yalla Ludo Diamond.

### 

How can I buy an Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card?

Once you have purchased an Yalla Ludo Diamond gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
 and [Riot Access USA](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/riot-access-usa/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

PUBG NEW STATE Mobile is a futuristic-style multiplayer online battle royale video game developed by PUBG Studios and published by Krafton. The game offers the intense battle royale experience of PUBG on mobile, new mode, new weapons, and exciting collaborations await!  

  
Buy PUBG New State Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1- Go to https://newstate.pubg.com/en/redemption Redemption Page.  
2-Enter the NC code received.  
3- Enter your game account ID.  
4- Redeem and enjoy!

### Terms and Conditions

Visit [https://www.pubgmobile.com/gamecredits/terms.html](https://www.pubgmobile.com/gamecredits/terms.html)

#### Pay with any payment method

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does PUBG New State accept Bitcoin or crypto?

PUBG New State does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an PUBG New State gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at PUBG New State.

### 

How can I buy an PUBG New State gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the PUBG New State gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your PUBG New State gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my PUBG New State gift card?

Once you have purchased an PUBG New State gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does The Fisherman Fishing Planet accept Bitcoin or crypto?

The Fisherman Fishing Planet does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at The Fisherman Fishing Planet.

### 

How can I buy an The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card?

Once you have purchased an The Fisherman Fishing Planet gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

MINECRAFT MINECOINS PACK - 1720 COINS Use Minecoins to purchase skins, textures packs, maps and more exciting content made by Minecraft community creators! Find new ways to play by visiting the in-game Minecraft Marketplace, where you’ll discover a constantly updating library of exciting new Minecraft content - from a community whose imagination knows no limits! Once you’ve redeemed your Minecoins, they’ll be linked with your Xbox Live account, so you can access your coins and purchases through all of your supported devices that run Minecraft.  

  
Buy Minecraft Minecoins Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

\*MINECOINS REQUIRE A VERSION OF MINECRAFT WITH MINECRAFT MARKETPLACE. UPDATES MAY BE REQUIRED. [MINECRAFT.NET/REDEEMCOINS](http://minecraft.net/REDEEMCOINS)
 To redeem code go to [minecraft.net/redeemcoins](http://minecraft.net/redeemcoins)
. Once redeemed to your Xbox Live account, the full code value will be applied and may be used for eligible purchases (exclusions apply) made directly at the Minecraft Marketplace.

### Terms and Conditions

NO CREDIT CARD REQUIRED, NO EXPIRATION. Eligible purchases and prices vary by region, device, and over time. Geography limitations, country and balance restrictions, taxes, and Internet connection fees may apply. Paid subscriptions required for some content. Age restrictions apply. Except as required by law, codes cannot be redeemed or exchanged for cash and are not refundable. To create a new Xbox Live account or to read full terms (which may change without notice), go to xbox.com/live.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Minecraft Minecoins accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Minecraft Minecoins does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Minecraft Minecoins gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Minecraft Minecoins.

### 

How can I buy an Minecraft Minecoins gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Minecraft Minecoins gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Minecraft Minecoins gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Minecraft Minecoins gift card?

Once you have purchased an Minecraft Minecoins gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

Hello Yo is the most popular live group voice talking and entertainment APP which you can create your free voice chat rooms and join others rooms.  
  
Meet new people, chat, sing with others, find game friends and send gifts to people nearby or around the world.

  
Buy Hello Yo Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Open your Hello Yo application.
2.  From your account profile select diamonds purchase.
3.  Click Recharge.
4.  Select your country from the drop-down menu.
5.  Select Mintroute as your payment option.
6.  Select denomination.
7.  Enter pin code printed on the receipt.

### Terms and Conditions

Once redeemed, Diamonds cannot be transferred between different Hello Yo accounts. For full legal terms, visit: [https://helloyo.sg/terms](https://helloyo.sg/terms)

#### That's it, ready to use it!

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Hello Yo accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Hello Yo does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Hello Yo gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Hello Yo.

### 

How can I buy an Hello Yo gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Hello Yo gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Hello Yo gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Hello Yo gift card?

Once you have purchased an Hello Yo gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Activitygift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/activitygift-us/)
, [Disney USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/disney-usa/)
, [Likee](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/likee-international/)
, [LiveMe Coins](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/liveme-coins-international/)
 and [OSN+ 6 Months Subscription](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/osn_-6-months-subscription-algeria/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

### Description

If you’re on Bitrefill, you probably know a thing or two about cryptocurrencies. What about your friends, family or colleagues?

At CoinEd, we believe that learning about this technology is essential for everyone, regardless of age or background. Since 2017, we've been dedicated to providing accurate and unbiased education that is simple, engaging and enjoyable.

Purchase a Bitrefill voucher for CoinEd’s flagship course and help share the borderless world of cryptocurrencies. With over 8 hours of content, students leave our course more digitally and financially literate with skills they can use to enhance their careers and lives.

Visit [coinedschool.com](https://coinedschool.com/)
 or email hello@CoinEdSchool.com for more information.

  
Buy CoinEd Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

After purchase, you will receive a 100% discount code to be used on our website during the checkout process.

1.  Purchase a Bitrefill voucher for CoinEd.
2.  Navigate to [coinedschool.com/bitrefill](https://coinedschool.com/bitrefill)
    
3.  Create an account during step 1 of checkout
4.  NB Enter your Bitrefill voucher code in the "Have a coupon?" field and click "Redeem"
5.  Your total will be discounted to $0
6.  Proceed with purchase

### Terms and Conditions

1.  Your discount code is only valid when using Paypal as the payment method
2.  Your discount code is only valid for new customers of CoinEd
3.  Your purchase is redeemable worldwide

For the full terms and conditions, or for assistance, visit [https://CoinEdSchool.com/terms](https://coinedschool.com/terms)
 or email hello@CoinEdSchool.com

#### Pay with any payment method

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does CoinEd accept Bitcoin or crypto?

CoinEd does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an CoinEd gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at CoinEd.

### 

How can I buy an CoinEd gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the CoinEd gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your CoinEd gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my CoinEd gift card?

Once you have purchased an CoinEd gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Bankless.com](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/bankless-international/)
, [Coinkite Bitcoin Wallets](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/coinkite-ca/)
, [CoinTracking](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/cointracking-international/)
, [Foundation Bitcoin Wallets](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/foundation-international/)
 and [OneKey USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/onekey-usd/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Kinguin is the premier destination for all your digital gaming needs. Established in 2013, it offer a curated selection that caters to the diverse tastes of the gaming community.

**Discover a World of Games**

*   **95,000+ Titles**: From casual puzzles to hardcore adventures, our extensive library ensures that every gamer finds something to love.
*   **Top Brands & Games**: Explore popular titles from leading brands like **FIFA**, **Call of Duty**, **Minecraft**, and **Assassin's Creed**. Buy subscriptions such as **Discord Nitro**, **Spotify** and **NordVPN**.

**Why Shop on Kinguin**

*   **Extensive Game Library**:Discover over 95,000 games, ranging from popular titles to unique indie gems. Whether you're a casual gamer or a hardcore enthusiast, Kinguin has something for everyone.
*   **Competitive Pricing**: Enjoy great savings with competitive prices, exclusive deals, and frequent discounts, making it easier to expand your game collection without breaking the bank.
*   **Instant Access**: Receive your game keys immediately after purchase, so you can start playing without any waiting time
*   **Comprehensive Gaming Essentials**: Shop for more than just games—find DLCs, character skins, and essential software to enhance your gaming experience.

Choosing the Kinguin Games Store via Bitrefill adds an additional layer of convenience. Paying with crypto allows instant access to your code, facilitating immediate immersion into your digital experience.

  
Buy Kinguin Games Store USD International Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Kinguin Games Store USD International accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Kinguin Games Store USD International does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Kinguin Games Store USD International.

### 

How can I buy an Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card?

Once you have purchased an Kinguin Games Store USD International gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

*   #1 Best-selling gift card for hotels since 2014
*   Stay at over 750,000 hotels worldwide
*   Hotels in 170+ countries
*   Buy and book instantly
*   Choose to personalise with a photo & message

You will receive a gift code and instructions for how to redeem the code on our website. It’s fast, easy and secure. Hotelgift is an Experiencegift brand.

  
Buy Hotelgift EUR Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Go to [https://www.hotelgift.com/](https://www.hotelgift.com/)
     and click on 'Redeem'
2.  Select one of over 750,000 hotels
3.  Enter your Hotelgift value code on the payment page
4.  Enjoy your hotel!

### Terms and Conditions

[https://www.hotelgift.com/terms-conditions/](https://www.hotelgift.com/terms-conditions)

*   This gift card can be redeemed worldwide.
*   This gift card is only redeemable on the e-commerce platform.
*   For **Flightgift** redemptions, customers can redeem **up to three (3) codes** during the checkout process.
*   For **Hotelgift** and other **Experiencegift** concepts, **only one (1) code** can be used during the checkout process.
*   If you have multiple codes for Hotelgift or other Experiencegift concepts, please contact the Hotelgift support team at [**support@experiencegift.com**](https://mailto:support@experiencegift.com/)
    . They will assist you in arranging the booking.

Anonymous

Oct 23, 2022

Worked as expected. I booked an IHG hotel, and did receive only a confirmation email by hotelgift platform (with a reference number only valid for their platform, not for IHG), so i did confirm my booking with the IHG support hotline to be sure. Also note that prices are pretty steep, compared to booking directly at the hotel (hotelgift takes a big share). Nevertheless, i will use the service again.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Hotelgift EUR accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Hotelgift EUR does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Hotelgift EUR gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Hotelgift EUR.

### 

How can I buy an Hotelgift EUR gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Hotelgift EUR gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Hotelgift EUR gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Hotelgift EUR gift card?

Once you have purchased an Hotelgift EUR gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Flightgift EUR](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flightgift-eu/)
, [Flightgift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flightgift-us/)
, [FlixBus EUR](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flixbus-international/)
, [FlixTrain EUR international](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flixtrain-international/)
 and [Hotelgift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/hotelgift-us/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does The Last Birdling accept Bitcoin or crypto?

The Last Birdling does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an The Last Birdling gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at The Last Birdling.

### 

How can I buy an The Last Birdling gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the The Last Birdling gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your The Last Birdling gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my The Last Birdling gift card?

Once you have purchased an The Last Birdling gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

Save the bankers is a campaign to preserve the splendid way of life of the bankers of Wall Street. Rest assured Every satoshi that you use will go undiluted to the bankers!  

  
Buy Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### Terms and Conditions

By making a donation to “Save the Bankers”, you are contributing to the fundraising campaign better explained [here](https://www.savethebankers.com/)
. This campaign seeks to collect charitable contributions to help the Bankers of Wall Street survive their upcoming doom brought about by the rise of cryptocurrencies. By donating via this page you are sending your coins directly to Bitrefill. 100% of the coins collected in this context will be used (in their fiat equivalent at the time of conversion - they prefer cash) to fund the endangered lifestyle of bankers. Your donation will be anonymous unless you specifically ask to be named. Your donation is definitive, will not be refunded, and by donating you expressly represent that you are aware of the intended destination of such donations and you agree with the goals of the campaign. We want to stress that despite any humorous undertones you may detect, both the donation request and the intention to give it to bankers are actual features of this campaign. ### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers.

### 

How can I buy an Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card?

Once you have purchased an Save the bankers - For False friends of the bankers gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.
