### How refills work

![](https://www.bitrefill.com/assets/bill-how-to-step-1-Bl4l2qlt.svg)

#### Enter a phone number & amount

Type in the phone number and the amount you want us to refill.

![](https://www.bitrefill.com/assets/bill-how-to-step-3-9453Ixri.svg)

#### Pay with any payment method

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

![](data:image/svg+xml,%3csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='86'%20height='63'%20fill='none'%3e%3crect%20width='78'%20height='55'%20x='6.73'%20y='1.48'%20fill='%23fff'%20stroke='%23002B28'%20stroke-width='2'%20rx='1'/%3e%3crect%20width='78'%20height='55'%20x='1'%20y='6.5'%20fill='%23fff'%20stroke='%23002B28'%20stroke-width='2'%20rx='1'/%3e%3crect%20width='12'%20height='12'%20x='10'%20y='15.5'%20fill='%23D7DCDA'%20rx='6'/%3e%3crect%20width='60'%20height='11'%20x='10'%20y='41.5'%20fill='%23D7DCDA'%20rx='2'/%3e%3ccircle%20cx='41'%20cy='33'%20r='20'%20fill='%23EA0B2C'/%3e%3cpath%20fill='%23fff'%20d='m46.5%2027.82-7.15%207.17-2.75-2.75a1.67%201.67%200%201%200-2.35%202.35l3.92%203.93a1.67%201.67%200%200%200%202.35%200l8.33-8.33a1.67%201.67%200%201%200-2.35-2.37Z'/%3e%3c/svg%3e)

#### That's it, here is your refill

Once your payment is confirmed you will get your refill sent out.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Djezzy accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Djezzy does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround that allows you to top up your smartphone with Bitcoin or other cryptocurrencies.

### 

How long does it take for the airtime top up to be received?

A mobile airtime top-up should be added to a phone number within a few seconds to minutes. Sometimes, there may be a small delay on the part of the mobile operator, but rest assured, we will send you an email confirmation as soon as your top-up has been processed successfully.

### 

What are some other Djezzy alternatives?

Some alternatives that customers consider in Algeria usually are [Ooredoo](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/recharge/ooredoo-algeria/)
 and [Mobilis](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/recharge/mobilis-algeria/)
. You can find many other options by visiting the [phone refill section](https://www.bitrefill.com/refill/?hl=en)
 on our website.

### 

I still have questions. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

### Description

•        Use the HiGift cards to purchase over 500 gift cards at HiGift.com •        Can be redeemed on payment checkout at HiGift.com •        It is available only to HiGift customers •        No returns or refunds on HiGift gift cards  

  
Buy HiGift Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

To redeem your gift card, follow these steps: 1.      Login into [https://higift.com](https://higift.com/)
 2.      Click on the +Payment tab on top of the page 3.      Click on “Redeem gift card” tab 4.      Enter your HiGift PIN to redeem your card

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does HiGift accept Bitcoin or crypto?

HiGift does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an HiGift gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at HiGift.

### 

How can I buy an HiGift gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the HiGift gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your HiGift gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my HiGift gift card?

Once you have purchased an HiGift gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

### Description

Eneba is a dynamic and user-friendly platform designed to meet all your gaming needs. It's a comprehensive marketplace that brings together a wide range of products and services under one virtual roof, making it a go-to destination for gamers worldwide.

For console enthusiasts, Eneba offers an extensive selection of games and accessories for popular systems such as **PlayStation**, **Xbox**, and **Nintendo Switch**. Whether you're a fan of action-packed adventures, thrilling sports games, or immersive RPGs, you'll find a game that suits your preferences.

PC gamers are not left out either. Eneba provides access to a vast library of games on renowned platforms like **Steam**, **Origin**, and **Riot Games**. From indie gems to blockbuster titles, the variety ensures there's something for everyone.

Moreover, Eneba understands the importance of in-game purchases in enhancing your gaming experience. That's why it offers a range of in-game currencies, including **Fortnite's Vbucks**, **GTA's Shark Cards**, and **FIFA's FUT points**, among others.

The platform also provides software products, including antivirus programs such as Norton and McAfee and operating systems, adding an extra layer of convenience for users.

In essence, Eneba is a comprehensive gaming marketplace that caters to a wide spectrum of needs. Whether you're looking for the latest games, in-game currencies, or software products, Eneba has got you covered.

  
Buy Eneba Games Store MXN Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Login to your account. If you don't have one yet, sign up.
2.  When logged in, click on your email address at the upper-right corner of the screen.
3.  Select “Redeem a gift card.”
4.  Enter the code in the box provided.
5.  Click Apply.

### Terms and Conditions

The following countries are not supported by Eneba and you will not be able to redeem your gift card: Crimea / Sevastopol, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Sudan, South Sudan, Syria, Bangladesh, Bolivia, Equatorial Guinea, Liberia, Namibia, Democratic Republic of the Congo, Afghanistan, Iraq, Myanmar, Pakistan, Palestine, Russia.

#### Pay with any payment method

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Eneba Games Store MXN accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Eneba Games Store MXN does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Eneba Games Store MXN gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Eneba Games Store MXN.

### 

How can I buy an Eneba Games Store MXN gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Eneba Games Store MXN gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Eneba Games Store MXN gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Eneba Games Store MXN gift card?

Once you have purchased an Eneba Games Store MXN gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does WebMoney WME accept Bitcoin or crypto?

WebMoney WME does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an WebMoney WME gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at WebMoney WME.

### 

How can I buy an WebMoney WME gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the WebMoney WME gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your WebMoney WME gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my WebMoney WME gift card?

Once you have purchased an WebMoney WME gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

Does Forza Horizon 4 accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Forza Horizon 4 does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Forza Horizon 4 gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Forza Horizon 4.

### 

How can I buy an Forza Horizon 4 gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Forza Horizon 4 gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Forza Horizon 4 gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Forza Horizon 4 gift card?

Once you have purchased an Forza Horizon 4 gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### How gift cards work

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Without Within 3 accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Without Within 3 does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Without Within 3 gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Without Within 3.

### 

How can I buy an Without Within 3 gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Without Within 3 gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Without Within 3 gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Without Within 3 gift card?

Once you have purchased an Without Within 3 gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

Introducing the Bitrefill Gift Card, a EUR denominated gift card, which can be spent on any of our digital vouchers or mobile refills, from anywhere in the world, instantly.

Bitrefill Gift Cards let you easily give the gift of Bitrefill, or top up your own Bitrefill Store Credits with a prepaid EUR credit which never expires, which you can spend on over 7000 brands, products, and services in 170 countries.

  
Buy Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Create a Bitrefill account or log in to your existing account
2.  Go to [https://www.bitrefill.com/account/redeem](https://www.bitrefill.com/account/redeem)
    
3.  Enter your code and redeem
4.  Now you're able to spend it on whatever product you'd like at Bitrefill using your Bitrefill Store Credits!

### Terms and Conditions

The Bitrefill Gift Cards are closed-loop prepaid instruments that allow a Customer to exclusively acquire goods or services sold on Bitrefill. Bitrefill Gift Cards are sold exclusively by Bitrefill and authorized resellers, can be denominated in USD or in EUR, and may not be used to buy other Bitrefill Gift Cards, either of the same or of a different denomination. If the value of a Bitrefill Gift Card is not enough to cover the order, the difference must be paid using any of the other accepted payment methods, or of an additional Bitrefill Gift Card. The value of Bitrefill Gift Cards will not in any case be reimbursed, paid out in cash, nor will it accrue interest. The Bitrefill Gift Cards can be applied to the corresponding Bitrefill Store Credits (denominated in USD or EUR, depending on the Bitrefill Gift Card being redeemed) or may be redeemable directly while concluding a purchase. This balance is non-refundable and may only be redeemed to acquire goods or services exclusively on Bitrefill. The Bitrefill Gift Cards have no expiration date and may be applied towards the Customer Bitrefill Store Credits at any time. Limitations of use. Each Bitrefill Gift Card can represent a credit of up to 1,500.00 EUR, or 2,000.00 USD at the time of sale. A Customer may not have, at any point, Bitrefill Store Credits, in aggregate, exceeding 10,000.00 USD. If, due to currency value fluctuating, a Balance surpasses such amount, the Customer will be asked to either spend the exceeding amount or provide necessary KYC information. If the Customer refuses, the Company reserves the right to deduct up to 2,000.00 USD from any of the Customer’s Bitrefill Store Credits and issue to the Customer’s registered email, a Bitrefill Gift Card in that amount. You are solely responsible for the safekeeping and security of your Bitrefill Gift Card following delivery. If you destroy or lose your Bitrefill Gift Card, or your Bitrefill Gift Card is stolen or used by someone else (with or without your permission), the Company shall not be liable for any loss or damage you suffer as a result. Certain Products, including products that allow for redemption in cryptocurrency, cannot be purchased by Bitrefill Gif Cards or the balances related thereto. \*Read the full the Bitrefill Terms and Conditions [here](https://www.bitrefill.com/terms)
.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR).

### 

How can I buy an Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card?

Once you have purchased an Bitrefill Gift Card (EUR) gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)

Private and Safe

### Description

PayPal is an online payment system that allows you to send and receive money around the world. PayPal Reward allows you to instantly send funds to a PayPal account holder. There are over 210 million active PayPal accounts worldwide, chances are good your recipients may already have one.

**Non-registered limits of 200 USD per card. Registered limits of 500 USD per card. Verified user limits of 1,000 USD per card, up to 10,000 USD per day.**

**Not all countries are supported, and some regions may only use PayPal to send payments and not receive payments. Before purchasing, services available for your country should be reviewed here:** [**https://www.paypal.com/webapps/mpp/country-worldwide**](https://www.paypal.com/webapps/mpp/country-worldwide)

**Please be aware that all purchases of this product are non-refundable.**

  
Buy PayPal USD Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Click the link received after purchase to be directed to the yourdigitalreward.com redemption website.
2.  Enter the email address that is registered with your PayPal account.
3.  If the email isn't linked to a PayPal account, you'll be prompted to set one up to access your funds.

### Terms and Conditions

By submitting this request, you are authorizing Your Digital Reward to provide personally identifiable information to PayPal, Inc. for the use of their services. Such personally identifiable information may include email address or phone number. This information is being shared to the extent that it is necessary for your use of PayPal services. If you submit incorrect information, Your Digital Reward has no ability to update your account information for a period of 30 days, per PayPal policy.

The availability of certain payment methods may be limited based on that particular seller or the third-party website you are using to complete the transaction.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does PayPal USD accept Bitcoin or crypto?

PayPal USD does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an PayPal USD gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at PayPal USD.

### 

How can I buy an PayPal USD gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the PayPal USD gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your PayPal USD gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my PayPal USD gift card?

Once you have purchased an PayPal USD gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

No Account Required

Instant Delivery

Private and Safe

### Description

Get unlimited access to over 100 high-quality games on Xbox One, Windows10 games plus Xbox Live Gold. With new games added all the time, Xbox Game Pass is your ticket to ongoing discovery.

If you want to see how much is left on the gift card, you can simply log in to your Microsoft account and navigate to the payment options section.

  
Buy Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

You can redeem your Xbox gift card online or on your Xbox console. Here is the process:

**Redeem Online:**

1.  Visit [**redeem.microsoft.com**](http://redeem.microsoft.com/)
     and sign in to your account.
2.  Enter your code and follow the instructions.

**Redeem on Xbox One or Xbox Series X/S:**

1.  Sign in and press the X button, then home, and go to Store.
2.  Select 'Use a Code'.
3.  Submit the 25-character code and follow the instructions.

**Redeem on Xbox 360:**

1.  Access your account.
2.  Click the Guide button on your controller.
3.  Go to Games & Apps and press 'Redeem code'.
4.  Enter the 25-character code of the Xbox Gift Card we have sent you and select 'Done'.
5.  Click 'Yes' to confirm.

### Terms and Conditions

1.  You can’t use Microsoft or Xbox gift cards to purchase content from the Xbox 360 Marketplace or Xbox 360 content on the Xbox One.
2.  When you purchase a Microsoft or Xbox gift card, make sure that the currency you use matches the currency associated with the recipient’s billing account. Otherwise, the recipient will be unable to redeem the gift card.
3.  If you redeem a Microsoft or Xbox gift card in a country that doesn’t match the country associated with your billing account, you won’t be able to use those funds.
4.  The funds in your Microsoft account can’t be transferred after you redeem a Microsoft or Xbox gift card.
    
    To know more, visit: [https://support.xbox.com/en-US/help/subscriptions-billing/redeem-codes-gifting/types-of-prepaid-codes](https://support.xbox.com/en-US/help/subscriptions-billing/redeem-codes-gifting/types-of-prepaid-codes)

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR.

### 

How can I buy an Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card?

Once you have purchased an Xbox Game Pass Ultimate EUR gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)

### Description

Liveme is an exciting entertainment platform that offers a unique way to connect with people around the world.

  
Buy LiveMe Coins Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Go to: [https://liveme.com](https://liveme.com/)
    
2.  Click on Recharge at the top right corner
3.  Login to your LiveMe account
4.  Select Mintroute as your payment option
5.  Select denomination
6.  Enter pin code printed on the receipt

### Terms and Conditions

Visit [https://www.liveme.com/protocol/terms.html](https://www.liveme.com/protocol/terms.html)

#### That's it, ready to use it!

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does LiveMe Coins accept Bitcoin or crypto?

LiveMe Coins does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an LiveMe Coins gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at LiveMe Coins.

### 

How can I buy an LiveMe Coins gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the LiveMe Coins gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your LiveMe Coins gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my LiveMe Coins gift card?

Once you have purchased an LiveMe Coins gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Activitygift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/activitygift-us/)
, [Disney USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/disney-usa/)
, [Hello Yo](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/hello-yo-international/)
, [Likee](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/likee-international/)
 and [OSN+ 6 Months Subscription](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/osn_-6-months-subscription-algeria/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

### Description

[G2A.com](https://www.g2a.com/)
 is a globally recognized digital marketplace known for its expansive catalog of amazing games at the most attractive prices. From globally appealing options to regional variants, G2A offers an incomparable online shopping experience for gaming enthusiasts.

*   **Steam, PSN, Xbox, Nintendo, Blizzard:** Use G2A for topping up your account for the most popular game stores.
*   **Gaming Gift Cards:** Find the best deals on various gaming gift cards on G2A.
*   **Game Keys and DLCs:** Discover the cheapest game keys and DLCs for your favorite games.
*   **Great customer experience**: 24-hour online Support, 100% Safety Guaranteed, Instant delivery.

When purchasing G2A products on Bitrefill with crypto, you enjoy many benefits. Get instant delivery of your discount code right after payment, enabling you to immediately use the discount code on G2A. You don't need an account to buy a G2A discount code. Enjoy the convenience of shopping on Bitrefill now.

  
Buy G2A Digital Marketplace Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

1.  Go to [G2A.com](http://g2a.com/)
     and log in to your account.
2.  Search for the game or digital item you want and add it to your cart.
3.  Open your cart and click Continue to payment.
4.  On the checkout page, find the field labeled “Discount code” or “Enter your code” below the order summary.
5.  Enter your discount code and click Apply.
6.  The discount will be applied to your order total.
7.  Choose your payment method and complete the purchase.

**Note:** Discount codes are single-use, and any unused value is forfeited. A credit card charge of at least USD 0.10 is required by G2A to complete checkout.

### Terms and Conditions

[https://www.g2a.com/terms-and-conditions](https://www.g2a.com/terms-and-conditions)

*   Each G2A discount code is **single-use only** and can be redeemed **once**.
*   Discount codes **cannot be partially used or reused**. If the value of the code is higher than your total checkout amount, **any remaining value will be lost** and cannot be applied to a future purchase.

*   Discount codes are **not gift cards** and do not add balance to your G2A account.

### Checkout & payment requirements

*   G2A requires a **credit card** to complete the checkout process.

*   When using a discount code, a **minimum credit card charge of USD 0.10** is required, even if the discount code covers the full value of your order.

*   This requirement is enforced by G2A’s checkout system, which always requires an additional payment method when redeeming discount codes.

### How gift cards work

#### That's it, ready to use it!

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does G2A Digital Marketplace accept Bitcoin or crypto?

G2A Digital Marketplace does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an G2A Digital Marketplace gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at G2A Digital Marketplace.

### 

How can I buy an G2A Digital Marketplace gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the G2A Digital Marketplace gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your G2A Digital Marketplace gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my G2A Digital Marketplace gift card?

Once you have purchased an G2A Digital Marketplace gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [PUBG Mobile UC](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/pubg-mobile/)
, [Steam USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/steam-usa/)
, [Roblox USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/roblox-usa/)
, [Yalla Ludo Diamond](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/yalla-ludo-diamond-international/)
 and [Mobile Legends Diamonds](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/mobile-legends-international/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.

---

### Description

The Hotels.com Gift Card is redeemable towards bookings at hundreds of thousands of places to stay in 200 countries and territories, ranging from international chains and all-inclusive resorts to local favorites and bed & breakfasts. Redeemable on Hotels.com, the Hotels.com Gift Card can be used in conjunction with member-only-deals and promotions. Bookings with the Hotels.com Gift Card count toward free nights with Hotels.com® Rewards where customers can earn a free\* night for every 10 nights stayed. For more information visit [www.hotels.com/giftcards](http://www.hotels.com/giftcards)
 or email [giftcards@hotels.com](https://mailto:giftcards@hotels.com/)
.

\*Subject to [Hotels.com](http://hotels.com/)
 Rewards terms and conditions, as set out at [www.hotels.com](http://www.hotels.com/)
.

  
Buy Hotels.com USD Gift Card with crypto such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Solana, Binance Pay and many more.

### How to Redeem

Redemption Instructions

1.  Visit [www.hotels.com/gc](https://www.hotels.com/gc)
    
2.  Search the destination and desired dates of travel
3.  Select the hotel and room type you wish to bookSelect "Pay Now" if applicable
4.  Enter your eGift Card number and PIN

Only one gift card can be redeemed per online booking, but multiple gift cards may be combined into one gift card with a maximum value of $2000 by visiting the balance transfer tab found at [www.hotels.com/gcbalance](https://www.hotels.com/gcbalance)
. If the amount of the booking exceeds the value of the gift card, additional payment will be due with a credit or debit card. When redeeming, hotel booking must be paid for in advance of arrival to the hotel by selecting the “Pay Now” option, instead of “Pay Later” at the hotel. Bookings are subject to availability and the hotel's terms and conditions.

A Gift Card cannot be used for:

*   Bookings paid for at the hotel
*   Bookings made over the phone
*   Package bookings i.e. hotel + flight
*   Bookings made through Group Travel Services
*   Bookings made prior to receipt of Gift Card

[https://hotels.jigsawbusinesssolutions.com/us/en-us/terms](https://hotels.jigsawbusinesssolutions.com/us/en-us/terms)

For full terms and conditions please visit their site directly as gift cards are not refundable

    .
*   Not redeemable at hotel locations or if you choose the Pay at Hotel option online.
*   Not redeemable toward existing bookings.
*   Not redeemable for Packages.

*   Not reloadable.
*   Safeguard the card. Not replaced if lost or stolen.

If delegated, the assignee, and not CARDCO, will be sole obligor to card owner. Card is distributed by Hotels.com. However, Hotels.com is not an obligor to card owner.
*   Purchase, use or acceptance of card constitutes acceptance of these terms.
*   For balance or other inquires visit [www.hotels.com/gcbalance](https://www.hotels.com/gcbalance)

#### Pay with any payment method

Your payment is confirmed the same minute in most cases.

#### That's it, ready to use it!

Redeem your card at your chosen retailer according to their instructions.

### Frequently asked questions

Check out our [Knowledge Base](https://help.bitrefill.com/)
 page for more FAQs

### 

Does Hotels.com USD accept Bitcoin or crypto?

Hotels.com USD does not accept crypto but Bitrefill provides a workaround by allowing you to purchase an Hotels.com USD gift card with Bitcoin or another cryptocurrency. This gift card can then be used to make purchases at Hotels.com USD.

### 

How can I buy an Hotels.com USD gift card with crypto?

1.  Enter the amount you want the Hotels.com USD gift card to have.
2.  Choose the cryptocurrency you want to use for payment, such as Bitcoin, Bitcoin Lightning, Ethereum, USDT, USDC, Litecoin, Dogecoin or Dash. Alternatively you can pay using Binance Pay.
3.  Once your payment is confirmed, you will get your Hotels.com USD gift card code.

### 

How long does it take to receive my Hotels.com USD gift card?

Once you have purchased an Hotels.com USD gift card at Bitrefill, it will be emailed to you almost instantly. Or you can redeem the gift card directly from the checkout page.

### 

What are some other types of gift cards that people commonly purchase?

Some great gift cards that people usually buy are [Flightgift EUR](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flightgift-eu/)
, [Flightgift USD](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flightgift-us/)
, [FlixBus EUR](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flixbus-international/)
, [FlixTrain EUR international](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/flixtrain-international/)
 and [Hotelgift EUR](https://www.bitrefill.com/dz/en/gift-cards/hotelgift-eu/)
. You can find a lot more options by visiting the [gift card section](https://www.bitrefill.com/us/en/)
.

### 

I have a question not answered here. How can I get help?

If you have a question that's not answered here, you can visit [our help center](https://bitrefill.zendesk.com/hc/en-us)
 and we'll be happy to assist you.
